name:S‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçr‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äçi

posted:Posted March 27, 2024
msg:Before coming to Anaya, I did some research, looked at several hotels and homestays, and after comprehensive comparison, I decided to come to Yinlu. The word Yinlu comes from "Gift to Zhao Yuelu" by Wei Zongwu of the Song Dynasty. Yinlu literally means a place of seclusion, and is often an elegant name for the residence of literati, showing their deep seclusion, elegant and quiet interests. Yinlu, located in Phase 8, is indeed relatively quiet.

As soon as I entered the hotel lobby, the service staff was very enthusiastic, helping with luggage, checking in, and informing about the tour. The front office manager Wu Haoyang took the initiative to provide various tour suggestions and provide the best choice.

We booked a twin room, which is spacious. The distance between the two beds is incomparable to that of ordinary hotels, and they do not interfere with each other when sleeping. The drinks, tea, coffee, and snacks provided in the hotel room are free. If you can't eat them, you can take them away. There is also a bathing pool in the shower room, providing coconut water, oranges, and bath salts. If you want to take a bath, you can ask the service staff to lay plastic sheets, which is more hygienic. If you don't want to take a bath, you can ask the customer service for a foot bath bucket, and they also provide foot bath bags. All of the above are free. The body lotion provided by the hotel is also very good and can be taken away.

I am very satisfied with the breakfast at Yinlu. It combines Chinese and Western styles, mainly Western breakfast. In addition, each person can choose a single item, which varies from day to day. Fried longli fish salad, Yuexuan salad bowl, wonton noodles, fried dumplings, all very good!

Finally, I have to thank the front desk manager of Yinlu. The travel route suggestions are very good, so that we can play without detours.

2. What dissatisfied us the most was that the child suddenly had a fever at night, so he asked the front desk for help and asked for help, but ended up going to the 24-hour owner's health center in Aranya, which is very close to the hotel, and the information was placed at the door (as shown in the picture) , at a glance. In addition, the hotel should also have some standing medicines for guests to use urgently. Most of the elderly and children who come to Aranya travel, the hotel should give full consideration to medical care, and provide practical information and timely assistance at the first time.

3. Although the hardware facilities of the hotel are good, the interior design and service of the room are very superficial. The family suite we stayed in was spacious but only had two small trash cans. Also, although there are two restrooms, one can only shower and one can only use the toilet. In addition, the slippers provided in the room rattled on the road, and the children had to rest and adults could only walk around the house barefoot at night.

4. There is only one restaurant in the hotel. It is understandable to put it in Aranya, but the overall feeling is that the restaurant of a five-star hotel is used as a training base for a junior hotel service school. From service to dress to catering quality, I dare not compliment. Although the restaurant is always full of waiters during business hours, no one will help you eat and collect the plates during breakfast. What you see is often a few waiters chatting nonchalantly and playing with their mobile phones: the other is the coffee machine There will always be a waiter standing next to you, making coffee for you, which is completely unnecessary. What's more, we stayed for a week, and the breakfast didn't change at all. Although there was a customized menu, every dining guest was not notified.

5. Again, the development of Aranya needs more excellent hotels and facilities, but the service also needs to keep up. The most satisfying thing about The Hermitage is its shuttle service, which is timely, convenient, and caring.
